## ראה (id: 006640000000000)

ראה
===

ראה (H7200 · H7202) — רַאֲוָה

verb · מַרְאֶה · מַרְאָה · רֹאֶה · רְאוּת · רְאִי · רֳאִי · הָרֹאֶה · יִרְאִיָּיה · רֹאֶה · רְאוּבֵן · רְאוּבֵנִי · רְאָיָה

See

to see, to look, to notice \= process or action by which living creatures perceive something, primarily \-\-though not necessarily exclusively\-\- with their eyes, either as a spontaneous incident or as the result of focusing the eyes on something

See

to be seen, to become visible, to appear \= process by which humans, deities, or objects become perceptible, primarily \-\-though not necessarily exclusively\-\- to the eye

## רָאָה (id: 006641000000000)

רָאָה
=====

רָאָה (H7201)

noun f

Birds

black kite \= bird of prey, dark brown with a greyish head and a long V\-shaped tail, flies relatively low and slowly; feeds on insects, frogs, lizards, and food scraps from human dwellings, and scavenge dead fish or other dead animals; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

[DEU 14:13](https://ref.ly/Deut14:13)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 14:13

## רֵאשׁ (id: 006653000000000)

רֵאשׁ
=====

רֵאשׁ (A7217)

noun m

head \= upper part of the human body, or the front or upper part of the body of an animal, typically separated from the rest of the body by a neck, and containing the brain, mouth, and sense organs

[DAN 2:28](https://ref.ly/Dan2:28) · [DAN 2:32](https://ref.ly/Dan2:32) · [DAN 2:38](https://ref.ly/Dan2:38) · [DAN 3:27](https://ref.ly/Dan3:27) · [DAN 4:2](https://ref.ly/Dan4:2) · [DAN 4:7](https://ref.ly/Dan4:7) · [DAN 4:10](https://ref.ly/Dan4:10) · [DAN 7:1](https://ref.ly/Dan7:1) · [DAN 7:6](https://ref.ly/Dan7:6) · [DAN 7:9](https://ref.ly/Dan7:9) · [DAN 7:15](https://ref.ly/Dan7:15) · [DAN 7:20](https://ref.ly/Dan7:20)

Leaders

head, chief, leader literally: head; hence: \= the person in leadership of a group of people, or, by extension, the most important object among a set of objects

[EZR 5:10](https://ref.ly/Ezra5:10)

Extraordinary

sum \= the parts of an event that is more important than other parts

[DAN 7:1](https://ref.ly/Dan7:1)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Daniel 2:28; Daniel 2:32; Daniel 2:38; Daniel 3:27; Daniel 4:2; Daniel 4:7; Daniel 4:10; Daniel 7:1; Daniel 7:6; Daniel 7:9; Daniel 7:15; Daniel 7:20; Ezra 5:10


## רֹאשׁ (id: 006654000000000)

רֹאשׁ
=====

רֹאשׁ (H7218 · H7219 · H7220)

noun m · מְרַאֲשֹׁות

head \= upper part of the human body, or the front or upper part of the body of an animal, typically separated from the rest of the body by a neck, and containing the brain, mouth, and sense organs; ≈ associated with the entire person, that person's life, and that person's responsibilities

Confident

**Collocation:** רום רֹאשׁ

one's head is lifted up \> to look up with confidence literally: (one's) head is lifted up; hence: \= state in which humans can look up without shame

[PSA 27:6](https://ref.ly/Ps27:6)

Confident

**Collocation:** רום רֹאשׁ

to lift up (one's) head \> to look up with confidence literally: to lift up (one's) head; hence: \= action by which humans look up without shame

[PSA 110:7](https://ref.ly/Ps110:7)

Confident

**Collocation:** רום רֹאשׁ

to lift up (someone's head) \> to cause (someone) to look up with confidence literally: to lift up (someone else's) head; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause humans to be able to look up without shame

[PSA 3:4](https://ref.ly/Ps3:4)

Conflict

**Collocation:** נשׂא רֹאשׁ

to be a threat literally: to lift up (one's) head; hence: \= action by which nations still have the ability to engage themselves in a military conflict with others, ◄ as someone who can still lift up his head after having been beaten down

[JDG 8:28](https://ref.ly/Judg8:28) · [PSA 83:3](https://ref.ly/Ps83:3) · [ZEC 2:4](https://ref.ly/Zech2:4)

Free

**Collocation:** נשׂא רֹאשׁ

to release from prison literally: to lift up (someone's) head; hence: \= causative action by which humans declare other humans free after having held them prisoner

[GEN 40:13](https://ref.ly/Gen40:13) · [GEN 40:20](https://ref.ly/Gen40:20) · [2KI 25:27](https://ref.ly/2Kgs25:27) · [JER 52:31](https://ref.ly/Jer52:31)

Frequency

count, sum literally: head; hence: \= the total number of a range of events

[PSA 119:160](https://ref.ly/Ps119:160) · [PSA 139:17](https://ref.ly/Ps139:17)

Good

best, finest \= literally: head; hence: \= state in which products have a quality that is superior to anything else

[EXO 30:23](https://ref.ly/Exod30:23) · [DEU 33:15](https://ref.ly/Deut33:15) · [SNG 4:14](https://ref.ly/Song4:14) · [EZK 27:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:22)

Intense

climax literally: head; hence: \= state in which an event reachest its highest level of intensity

[PSA 137:6](https://ref.ly/Ps137:6)

Leaders

head, chief, leader literally: head; hence: \= the person in leadership of a group of people, or, by extension, the most important object among a set of objects

Spatial Referents

top, peak, head literally: head; hence: \= a referent pointing to the topmost part of a vertically oriented object, such as a mountain, and the principal part of an horizontally oriented object, such as a street or a bed

## רֹאשָׁה (id: 006656000000000)

רֹאשָׁה
=======

רֹאשָׁה (H7222)

adj · רֹאשׁ

Buildings

**Collocation:** אֶבֶן ראֹשָׁה

headstone \= exact meaning unsure; literally: head stone; hence: \= the highest stone in a construction, which, in this context, may either refer to the foundation of a previous construction on which a new construction is to be erected, or to the capstone that completes a new construction

[ZEC 4:7](https://ref.ly/Zech4:7)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Zechariah 4:7

## רַב (id: 006660000000000)

רַב
===

## רבב (id: 006662000000000)

רבב
===

רבב (H7231 · H7232)

verb · רַב · רֹב · רְבִיבִים · רבה · מֵרַב

Quantity · Frequency

to multiply, to become numerous \= process by which people, objects, and events increase in number or frequency

[GEN 6:1](https://ref.ly/Gen6:1) · [EXO 23:29](https://ref.ly/Exod23:29) · [DEU 7:7](https://ref.ly/Deut7:7) · [1SA 25:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam25:10) · [JOB 35:6](https://ref.ly/Job35:6) · [PSA 3:2](https://ref.ly/Ps3:2) · [PSA 4:8](https://ref.ly/Ps4:8) · [PSA 25:19](https://ref.ly/Ps25:19) · [PSA 38:20](https://ref.ly/Ps38:20) · [PSA 69:5](https://ref.ly/Ps69:5) · [PSA 104:24](https://ref.ly/Ps104:24) · [ECC 5:10](https://ref.ly/Eccl5:10) · [ISA 6:12](https://ref.ly/Isa6:12) · [ISA 22:9](https://ref.ly/Isa22:9) · [ISA 59:12](https://ref.ly/Isa59:12) · [ISA 66:16](https://ref.ly/Isa66:16) · [JER 5:6](https://ref.ly/Jer5:6) · [JER 14:7](https://ref.ly/Jer14:7) · [JER 46:23](https://ref.ly/Jer46:23) · [HOS 4:7](https://ref.ly/Hos4:7)

Intense

## רְבָבָה (id: 006663000000000)

רְבָבָה
=======

רְבָבָה (H7233)

noun f · רבב

## רגז (id: 006685000000000)

רגז
===

רגז (H7264 · A7265)

verb · אַרְגַּז · רַגָּז · רֹגֶז · רָגְזָה

Unsteady

to tremble, to shake, to quake, to be disturbed, to be perturbed, to be excited, to flutter \= process by which humans or objects shake involuntarily; ◄ typically as a result of fear, insecurity, shock, excitement, or other emotions

[EXO 15:14](https://ref.ly/Exod15:14) · [DEU 2:25](https://ref.ly/Deut2:25) · [1SA 14:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:15) · [2SA 7:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:10) · [2SA 19:1](https://ref.ly/2Sam19:1) · [2SA 22:8](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:8) · [1CH 17:9](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:9) · [PSA 4:5](https://ref.ly/Ps4:5) · [PSA 18:8](https://ref.ly/Ps18:8) · [PSA 77:17](https://ref.ly/Ps77:17) · [PSA 77:19](https://ref.ly/Ps77:19) · [PSA 99:1](https://ref.ly/Ps99:1) · [PRO 30:21](https://ref.ly/Prov30:21) · [ISA 5:25](https://ref.ly/Isa5:25) · [ISA 32:10](https://ref.ly/Isa32:10) · [ISA 32:11](https://ref.ly/Isa32:11) · [ISA 64:1](https://ref.ly/Isa64:1) · [JER 33:9](https://ref.ly/Jer33:9) · [JOL 2:1](https://ref.ly/Joel2:1) · [JOL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Joel2:10) · [AMO 8:8](https://ref.ly/Amos8:8) · [MIC 7:17](https://ref.ly/Mic7:17) · [HAB 3:7](https://ref.ly/Hab3:7) · [HAB 3:16](https://ref.ly/Hab3:16) · [HAB 3:16](https://ref.ly/Hab3:16)

to shake, to make tremble, to disturb \= causative action by which humans or deities cause (other) humans or objects to shake; ◄ typically as a result of fear, insecurity, shock, excitement, or other emotions

to lift one's foot \> to do anything at all literally: (to raise one's) foot; hence: \= to do anything, even if it were as insignificant as raising one's foot

Excrete

**Collocation:** סכך רַגְלַיִם

to cover the feet a euphemism; literally: to cover (one's) feet; hence: \= action by which humans pass excrement, ◄ which implies a squatting position by which the robe covers the feet

Move

step literally: foot; hence: \= action by which humans put one foot before the other ► in order to move forward

Move

## רוּחַ (id: 006724000000000)

רוּחַ
=====

רוּחַ (H7307 · A7308)

noun f

Deities

Spirit \= an invisible being that is in a direct relation to and under control of God and one of his manifestation, often described as a substance that can be poured out, ► through whom the universe is created and animated; it can manifest itself as an invisible force equipping humans with wisdom, skill, and strength for specific tasks; it can also manifest itself as a movement of air through the bodies of animate creatures (breath) or through nature (wind)

spirit \= an invisible being associated with God and carrying out his commands, often by taking possession of people and influencing their actions

People

(human) spirit, mind \= inner person of a human or celestial being, associated with emotions, such as joy, grief, worry, courage, anger, willingness, jealousy, etc., but also with inner qualities such as wisdom

Air

breeze, wind \= a natural movement of air, blowing in a particular direction, ranging in intensity from a light breeze ([JOB 41:8](https://ref.ly/Job41:8)) to a heavy blast ([JOB 1:19](https://ref.ly/Job1:19)); ≈ often regarded as the breath of God, but also associated with things that are without substance and cannot be grasped

Chastise

breath \> punishment literally: (God's) breath; hence: \= process by which humans are punished by God, ◄ described as a flaming breath coming from his mouth

[JOB 4:9](https://ref.ly/Job4:9) · [JOB 15:30](https://ref.ly/Job15:30) · [ISA 11:4](https://ref.ly/Isa11:4) · [ISA 11:15](https://ref.ly/Isa11:15) · [ISA 30:28](https://ref.ly/Isa30:28)

Non\-Endure

breath \> fleeting literally: breath or wind; hence: \= state in which an event does not last, but is over before one knows it

[JOB 7:7](https://ref.ly/Job7:7)

Fail

empty words literally: breath or wind; hence: \= action by which humans speak words with no substance or value

[JOB 6:26](https://ref.ly/Job6:26) · [JOB 8:2](https://ref.ly/Job8:2) · [JOB 15:2](https://ref.ly/Job15:2) · [JOB 16:3](https://ref.ly/Job16:3) · [MIC 2:11](https://ref.ly/Mic2:11)

Spatial Referents

direction literally: wind; \= one of the four quarters of heaven, ◄ associated with the wind ► used for orientation purposes

[1CH 9:24](https://ref.ly/1Chr9:24) · [JER 49:32](https://ref.ly/Jer49:32) · [JER 49:36](https://ref.ly/Jer49:36) · [JER 49:36](https://ref.ly/Jer49:36) · [JER 52:23](https://ref.ly/Jer52:23) · [EZK 12:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek12:14) · [EZK 17:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek17:21) · [EZK 37:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:9) · [EZK 42:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:16) · [EZK 42:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:17) · [EZK 42:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:18) · [EZK 42:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:19) · [EZK 42:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:20) · [DAN 7:2](https://ref.ly/Dan7:2) · [DAN 8:8](https://ref.ly/Dan8:8) · [DAN 11:4](https://ref.ly/Dan11:4) · [ZEC 2:10](https://ref.ly/Zech2:10)

Speak

**Collocation:** רוּחַ פֶּה

breath of mouth \> words literally: the breath of (one's) mouth; hence: \= action by which humans utter words ◄ which are articulated with the help of the breath which leaves the body through the mouth

[PSA 33:6](https://ref.ly/Ps33:6)

Blow

breath \= the air that is taken in and expelled through the lungs by humans and animals, which makes them live, and which distinguishes them from inanimate objects like idols; ≈ regarded as coming from God; sometimes God is depicted as a breathing being as well

## רֶוַח (id: 006725000000000)

רֶוַח
=====

רֶוַח (H7305)

noun m · רוח

Space

space, distance \= an amount of space between two objects

[GEN 32:17](https://ref.ly/Gen32:17)

Relief

relief literally: space; hence: \= process by which humans find relief after a period of hardship

[EST 4:14](https://ref.ly/Esth4:14)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 32:17; Esther 4:14

## רושׁ (id: 006738000000000)

רושׁ
====

רושׁ (H7326)

verb · רֵישׁ

Non\-Possess

to suffer want \= state in which an animal lacks what is essential for its normal needs

[PSA 34:11](https://ref.ly/Ps34:11)

Poor

poor, destitute \= state of being needy as a result of one's lack of monetary or physical resources, usually resulting in a lower social status with little authority or power and at the risk of being exploited

[1SA 18:23](https://ref.ly/1Sam18:23) · [2SA 12:1](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:1) · [2SA 12:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:3) · [2SA 12:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:4) · [PSA 82:3](https://ref.ly/Ps82:3) · [PRO 13:8](https://ref.ly/Prov13:8) · [PRO 13:23](https://ref.ly/Prov13:23) · [PRO 14:20](https://ref.ly/Prov14:20) · [PRO 17:5](https://ref.ly/Prov17:5) · [PRO 18:23](https://ref.ly/Prov18:23) · [PRO 19:1](https://ref.ly/Prov19:1) · [PRO 19:7](https://ref.ly/Prov19:7) · [PRO 19:22](https://ref.ly/Prov19:22) · [PRO 22:2](https://ref.ly/Prov22:2) · [PRO 22:7](https://ref.ly/Prov22:7) · [PRO 28:3](https://ref.ly/Prov28:3) · [PRO 28:6](https://ref.ly/Prov28:6) · [PRO 28:27](https://ref.ly/Prov28:27) · [PRO 29:13](https://ref.ly/Prov29:13) · [ECC 4:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl4:14) · [ECC 5:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl5:7)

Poor

to pretend to be poor \= action by which humans behave as if they are poor and lack resources

[PRO 10:4](https://ref.ly/Prov10:4) · [PRO 13:7](https://ref.ly/Prov13:7)

Steve Berneking

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 34:11; 1 Samuel 18:23; 2 Samuel 12:1; 2 Samuel 12:3; 2 Samuel 12:4; Psalms 82:3; Proverbs 13:8; Proverbs 13:23; Proverbs 14:20; Proverbs 17:5; Proverbs 18:23; Proverbs 19:1; Proverbs 19:7; Proverbs 19:22; Proverbs 22:2; Proverbs 22:7; Proverbs 28:3; Proverbs 28:6; Proverbs 28:27; Proverbs 29:13; Ecclesiastes 4:14; Ecclesiastes 5:7; Proverbs 10:4; Proverbs 13:7

## רזה (id: 006741000000000)

רזה
===

רזה (H7329)

verb · רָזֶה · רָזֹון · רָזִי

Thin

to grow lean, to waste away \= process by which humans lose flesh or fat on their body; ≈ used figuratively to denote how a nation loses its wealth and prosperity

[ISA 17:4](https://ref.ly/Isa17:4)

Thin

to cause to waste away literally: to cause to grow lean; hence: \= causative process by which humans cause other humans to lose flesh or fat on their body ◄ by withholding food; ≈ used figuratively ro denote a situation in which idols are no longer sacrificed to, as a result of which they waste away

[ZEP 2:11](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:11)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 17:4; Zephaniah 2:11

## רחב (id: 006748000000000)

רחב
===

רחב (H7337)

verb · מֶרְחָב · רָחָב · רַחַב · רֹחַב · רְחֹב

Large

to be large, to be broad \= state in which an object is large in size

[ISA 30:23](https://ref.ly/Isa30:23)

Large

to become larger \= state in which one object has a relatively large distance from side to side compared to another, similar object

[EZK 41:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek41:7)

Large

to enlarge, to make large \= causative action by which humans or deities increase the size of an area or object

[EXO 34:24](https://ref.ly/Exod34:24) · [DEU 12:20](https://ref.ly/Deut12:20) · [DEU 19:8](https://ref.ly/Deut19:8) · [DEU 33:20](https://ref.ly/Deut33:20) · [ISA 30:33](https://ref.ly/Isa30:33) · [ISA 54:2](https://ref.ly/Isa54:2) · [ISA 57:8](https://ref.ly/Isa57:8) · [AMO 1:13](https://ref.ly/Amos1:13) · [MIC 1:16](https://ref.ly/Mic1:16)

Intense

**Collocation:** רחב נֶפֶשׁ

to enlarge (one's) self \> to be excessively greedy literally: to make large one's self; hence: \= causative process by which humans act with intense greed

[HAB 2:5](https://ref.ly/Hab2:5)

Rejoice

**Collocation:** לֵבָב רחב

(one's) heart is enlarged \> to be full of joy literally: (one's) heart is open wide; hence: \= state in which humans experience an abundance of joy

[ISA 60:5](https://ref.ly/Isa60:5)

Relief

to enlarge \> to ease (someone's circumstances) literally: to enlarge (for someone); hence: \= causative action by which humans or deities grant relief to (other) humans by alleviating difficult circumstances

[GEN 26:22](https://ref.ly/Gen26:22) · [PSA 4:2](https://ref.ly/Ps4:2) · [PRO 18:16](https://ref.ly/Prov18:16)

Relief

**Collocation:** רחב צָרָה

to grant relief from troubles, to ease troubles literally: to enlarge narrow things; hence: \= causative action by which deities grant relief to humans by alleviating difficult circumstances

[PSA 25:17](https://ref.ly/Ps25:17)

Stance

**Collocation:** רחב נֶפֶשׁ

to open wide (one's) gullet literally: to enlarge (one's) gullet; \= action by which a place prepares itself for a large group of people ◄ as if it were an animal that opens its mouth wide to swallow a large quantity of food

[ISA 5:14](https://ref.ly/Isa5:14)

Stance

**Collocation:** פֶּה רחב

to be wide open \= state in which humans have their mouth wide open

[1SA 2:1](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:1)

Stance

**Collocation:** רחב פֶּה

to open wide (one's) mouth \= action by which humans open their mouth widely in order to put out one's tongue, to be fed, or to shout

[PSA 35:21](https://ref.ly/Ps35:21) · [PSA 81:11](https://ref.ly/Ps81:11) · [ISA 57:4](https://ref.ly/Isa57:4)

Succeed

**Collocation:** רחב צַעָד

to enlarge (someone's) steps \> to clear the way (for someone) literally: to enlarge (someone's) steps; hence: \= causative action by which deities make humans successful in their undertakings

[2SA 22:37](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:37) · [PSA 18:37](https://ref.ly/Ps18:37)

Wise

**Collocation:** רחב לֵב

to enlarge (someone's heart) \> to broaden (someone's) understanding literally: to enlarge (someone's) heart; hence: \= causative action by which deities grant wisdom and understanding to humans

[PSA 119:32](https://ref.ly/Ps119:32)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 30:23; Ezekiel 41:7; Exodus 34:24; Deuteronomy 12:20; Deuteronomy 19:8; Deuteronomy 33:20; Isaiah 30:33; Isaiah 54:2; Isaiah 57:8; Amos 1:13; Micah 1:16; Habakkuk 2:5; Isaiah 60:5; Genesis 26:22; Psalms 4:2; Proverbs 18:16; Psalms 25:17; Isaiah 5:14; 1 Samuel 2:1; Psalms 35:21; Psalms 81:11; Isaiah 57:4; 2 Samuel 22:37; Psalms 18:37; Psalms 119:32

far, distant (from someone) literally: far (from someone else); hence: \= state in which deities are no longer associating with humans, ◄ as if they have distanced themselves

far (from doing something) literally: (to be) far (from an action); hence: \= state in which deities do not seem to be willing or able to engage in any way

(an event is) far, elusive literally: (an event is) far (from someone); hence: \= state in which it seems unlikely for humans to experience a certain event

## רָחָם (id: 006767000000000)

רָחָם
=====

רָחָם (H7360) — רָחָמָה

noun m

Birds

Egyptian vulture \= relatively small type of vulture with a long, untidy, light orange\-brown feathers on its neck and head, a bare yellow face, and a yellow beak that is longer and less hooked than most vultures; the rest of the body and wings are white with black wing tips; it feeds on the scraps of carrion dropped by larger vultures, since its beak is not strong enough to tear skin and meat easily; usually scavenges scraps on beaches or rubbish dumps and eats the eggs of ground\-nesting waterside birds such as plovers, sandpipers, curlews, and others, which it breaks by knocking them with a large stone; ◄ Neophron percnopterus; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

[LEV 11:18](https://ref.ly/Lev11:18) · [DEU 14:17](https://ref.ly/Deut14:17)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 11:18; Deuteronomy 14:17

[ISA 1:6](https://ref.ly/Isa1:6)

Afraid

**Collocation:** לֵבָב רכך

to be timid literally: (one's) heart is soft; hence: \= process by which humans lose courage

רכל

רכל (H7402)

verb · מַרְכֹּלֶת · רָכִיל · רְכֻלָּה

Exchange

to trade \= action by which humans engage in commercial activity by which merchandise and goods are traded, or bought and sold, with the intention of making a profit

[EZK 27:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:13) · [EZK 27:15](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:15) · [EZK 27:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:17) · [EZK 27:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:20) · [EZK 27:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:22) · [EZK 27:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:23) · [EZK 27:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:24)

Professions

trader \= a person whose profession it is to engage in commercial activity by which merchandise and goods are traded, or bought and sold, with the intention of making a profit

[1KI 10:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs10:15) · [NEH 3:31](https://ref.ly/Neh3:31) · [NEH 3:32](https://ref.ly/Neh3:32) · [NEH 13:20](https://ref.ly/Neh13:20) · [SNG 3:6](https://ref.ly/Song3:6) · [EZK 17:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek17:4) · [EZK 27:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:3) · [EZK 27:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:22) · [EZK 27:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:23) · [NAM 3:16](https://ref.ly/Nah3:16)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Ezekiel 27:13; Ezekiel 27:15; Ezekiel 27:17; Ezekiel 27:20; Ezekiel 27:22; Ezekiel 27:23; Ezekiel 27:24; 1 Kings 10:15; Nehemiah 3:31; Nehemiah 3:32; Nehemiah 13:20; Song of Songs 3:6; Ezekiel 17:4; Ezekiel 27:3; Nahum 3:16

Swarming Creatures

worm, maggot \= small, soft, legless, tube\-shaped creatures that have no bones or shells; they typically feed on overripe fruit, rotting meat, and similar things; most are larvae that hatch from the eggs laid by flies or some beetles; associated with uncleanness, mortality, decay, and death

## רִמֹּון (id: 006825000000000)

רִמֹּון
=======

רִמֹּון (H7416)

noun m · עֵין רִמֹּון

Trees · Fruits

pomegranate \= a small tree reaching a height of 3–5 m, with narrow, dark green leaves and thorny branches; its has a red flower and produces red round fruits with a hard skin and tightly\-packed pockets of seeds inside; ◄ Punica granatum; ► the seeds can be made into wine; the flower\-shaped end of the fruit made it an attractive decoration on stone and in the temple; ≈ associated with love, beauty, and sex

## רֹמַח (id: 006829000000000)

רֹמַח
=====

רֹמַח (H7420) [SAHD](SAHD@http://www.sahd.div.ed.ac.uk/_media/lexeme:pdf:ebt-chenit-williams_p-cam-1998p.pdf)

noun m

Weapons

spear \= a long, straight rod, usually made of wood, with a sharp iron head or point; used for piercing by thrusting; its length varied from the height of a man to much longer There is strong semantic overlap with synonym חֲנִית.

## רְנָנִים (id: 006846000000000)

רְנָנִים
========

רְנָנִים (H7443)

noun m · רנן

Birds

ostrich \= large bird with underdeveloped wings so that itcannot fly; it has a long neck and long legs and is about 2 meters tall; its head and neck are almost bald, being covered in short bristles; the male's body is black with long white feathers on its wings; its tail is white, gray, or light brown; the females are a uniform grayish brown; they feed mainly on seeds, fallen fruit, and shoots and may occasionally eat a lizard or a frog; they live in small flocks of about twenty, of which four or five are males; as many as ten females may lay their eggs in the one nest, but only one female and one male will incubate the eggs, with the female on the nest in the daytime, and the male taking over later in the afternoon; male ostriches make a series of deep booming hoots that can be heard great distances and which are often mistaken for the roar of a lion; ◄ \|iStruthio camelus; \|i\*≈ associated with heartless cruelty because most females do not hatch their own eggs and do not take care of their own young

[JOB 39:13](https://ref.ly/Job39:13)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 39:13

## רַע (id: 006852000000000)

רַע
===

רַע (H7451a · H7451b) — רָע

adj · רעע

## רֹעַ (id: 006853000000000)

רֹעַ
====

רֹעַ (H7455)

noun m · רעע

Bad

bad, ugly \= condition of an object that is of such poor quality that it can be observed or evaluated externally

[GEN 41:19](https://ref.ly/Gen41:19) · [JER 24:2](https://ref.ly/Jer24:2) · [JER 24:3](https://ref.ly/Jer24:3) · [JER 24:8](https://ref.ly/Jer24:8) · [JER 29:17](https://ref.ly/Jer29:17)

Grieve

**Collocation:** רֹעַ לֵב

sadness literally: badness of heart; hence: \= state in which humans experience an emotion of sadness, often visible in their facial expression

[NEH 2:2](https://ref.ly/Neh2:2)

Grieve

**Collocation:** רֹעַ פָּנִים

sadness literally: badness of face; hence: \= state in which humans experience an emotion of sadness, often visible in their facial expression

[ECC 7:3](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:3)

Wrong

evil, wickedness, wrong \= state in which an event is morally and/or ethically wrong

[DEU 28:20](https://ref.ly/Deut28:20) · [1SA 17:28](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:28) · [PSA 28:4](https://ref.ly/Ps28:4) · [ISA 1:16](https://ref.ly/Isa1:16) · [JER 4:4](https://ref.ly/Jer4:4) · [JER 21:12](https://ref.ly/Jer21:12) · [JER 23:2](https://ref.ly/Jer23:2) · [JER 23:22](https://ref.ly/Jer23:22) · [JER 25:5](https://ref.ly/Jer25:5) · [JER 26:3](https://ref.ly/Jer26:3) · [JER 44:22](https://ref.ly/Jer44:22) · [HOS 9:15](https://ref.ly/Hos9:15)

Steve Berneking

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 41:19; Jeremiah 24:2; Jeremiah 24:3; Jeremiah 24:8; Jeremiah 29:17; Nehemiah 2:2; Ecclesiastes 7:3; Deuteronomy 28:20; 1 Samuel 17:28; Psalms 28:4; Isaiah 1:16; Jeremiah 4:4; Jeremiah 21:12; Jeremiah 23:2; Jeremiah 23:22; Jeremiah 25:5; Jeremiah 26:3; Jeremiah 44:22; Hosea 9:15


## רעב (id: 006854000000000)

רעב
===

רעב (H7456)

verb · רָעָב · רָעֵב · רְעָבֹון

Hunger

to be hungry, to starve \= state in which humans are wanting or needing food, but having little to no access to it

[GEN 41:55](https://ref.ly/Gen41:55) · [PSA 34:11](https://ref.ly/Ps34:11) · [PSA 50:12](https://ref.ly/Ps50:12) · [PRO 6:30](https://ref.ly/Prov6:30) · [PRO 19:15](https://ref.ly/Prov19:15) · [ISA 8:21](https://ref.ly/Isa8:21) · [ISA 9:19](https://ref.ly/Isa9:19) · [ISA 44:12](https://ref.ly/Isa44:12) · [ISA 49:10](https://ref.ly/Isa49:10) · [ISA 65:13](https://ref.ly/Isa65:13) · [JER 42:14](https://ref.ly/Jer42:14)

Hunger

to cause hunger, to let (one) go hungry \= causative action by which a person is kept from having access to food

[DEU 8:3](https://ref.ly/Deut8:3) · [PRO 10:3](https://ref.ly/Prov10:3)

Steve Berneking

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 41:55; Psalms 34:11; Psalms 50:12; Proverbs 6:30; Proverbs 19:15; Isaiah 8:21; Isaiah 9:19; Isaiah 44:12; Isaiah 49:10; Isaiah 65:13; Jeremiah 42:14; Deuteronomy 8:3; Proverbs 10:3


## רָעֵב (id: 006855000000000)

רָעֵב
=====

רָעֵב (H7457)

adj · רעב

Hunger

hungry \= condition of not having food to eat, often leading to weakness

## רָעָב (id: 006856000000000)

רָעָב
=====

רָעָב (H7458)

noun m · רעב

Hunger

hunger, famine \= state of having a lack of food for a period of time, affecting an individual for a short time or a large number of people in a geographical area for a prolonged time (as in famine)

רְעָבֹון

noun m · רעב

Engage

Move

רפד (H7502)

verb · רְפִידָה

Dead

**Collocation:** רפד יָצוּעַ בַּחֹשֶׁךְ

to make one's bed in darkness literally: to spreak (one's) bed in darkness; hence: \= process by which humans die and move to the world of the dead

[JOB 17:13](https://ref.ly/Job17:13)

Stance

to spread oneself \= action by which animals assume a lying position

[JOB 41:22](https://ref.ly/Job41:22)

verb · רְפִידָה

Strong

to refresh \= causative action by which humans help other humans to regain their strength

[SNG 2:5](https://ref.ly/Song2:5)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 17:13; Job 41:22; Song of Songs 2:5

רפה

Weak

to discourage literally: to make (someone's) hands weak; hence: \= causative process by which humans cause other humans to lose courage and unable to perform as they should

to be slack \= state in which humans fail to engage in an activity

Non\-Engage

to leave, to give up, to let go \= action by which humans or deities refrain from an activity

Non\-Engage

to leave (someone) alone \= action by which humans or deities refrain from an activity affecting another person

Insignificant

**Collocation:** רפה מְזִיחַ

to loosen (someone's) belt \> to disgrace (someone) literally: to loosen (someone's) belt; hence: \= causative process by which deities cause humans to lose power and status

[JOB 12:21](https://ref.ly/Job12:21)

Lazy

to be lazy, to be idle literally: to loosen oneself; hence: \= state in which humans are reluctant to work or make an effort

[EXO 5:8](https://ref.ly/Exod5:8) · [EXO 5:17](https://ref.ly/Exod5:17) · [EXO 5:17](https://ref.ly/Exod5:17)

Unfaithful

**Collocation:** רפה יָד

to abandon literally: to loosen (one's) hand; hence: \= action by which humans suspend their commitment to other humans

Unfaithful

[ISA 5:24](https://ref.ly/Isa5:24)

acceptance, favor \= state in which deities or humans in a position of authority are favorable disposed towards a person or activity

Willing

acceptance \= state in which a person who offers something as a sacrifice is considered acceptable to the receiver, together with the sacrifice itself

[EXO 28:38](https://ref.ly/Exod28:38) · [LEV 1:3](https://ref.ly/Lev1:3) · [LEV 19:5](https://ref.ly/Lev19:5) · [LEV 22:19](https://ref.ly/Lev22:19) · [LEV 22:20](https://ref.ly/Lev22:20) · [LEV 22:21](https://ref.ly/Lev22:21) · [LEV 22:29](https://ref.ly/Lev22:29) · [LEV 23:11](https://ref.ly/Lev23:11) · [PSA 19:15](https://ref.ly/Ps19:15) · [ISA 56:7](https://ref.ly/Isa56:7) · [ISA 60:7](https://ref.ly/Isa60:7) · [JER 6:20](https://ref.ly/Jer6:20) · [MAL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Mal2:13)

## רִשְׁעָה (id: 006953000000000)

רִשְׁעָה
========

רִשְׁעָה (H7564)

noun f

Sin

wicked deeds, wickedness \= action by which humans act in a way that is contrary to (God's) law, ► resulting in a state of guilt

[DEU 9:4](https://ref.ly/Deut9:4) · [DEU 9:5](https://ref.ly/Deut9:5) · [DEU 25:2](https://ref.ly/Deut25:2) · [PRO 11:5](https://ref.ly/Prov11:5) · [PRO 13:6](https://ref.ly/Prov13:6) · [ISA 9:17](https://ref.ly/Isa9:17) · [EZK 5:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek5:6) · [EZK 18:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:20) · [EZK 18:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:27) · [EZK 33:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:12) · [EZK 33:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:19) · [ZEC 5:8](https://ref.ly/Zech5:8) · [MAL 1:4](https://ref.ly/Mal1:4) · [MAL 3:15](https://ref.ly/Mal3:15) · [MAL 3:19](https://ref.ly/Mal3:19)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 9:4; Deuteronomy 9:5; Deuteronomy 25:2; Proverbs 11:5; Proverbs 13:6; Isaiah 9:17; Ezekiel 5:6; Ezekiel 18:20; Ezekiel 18:27; Ezekiel 33:12; Ezekiel 33:19; Zechariah 5:8; Malachi 1:4; Malachi 3:15; Malachi 3:19


## רֶשֶׁף (id: 006954000000000)

רֶשֶׁף
======

רֶשֶׁף (H7565 · H7566)

noun m

Fire

**Collocation:** בְּנֵי־רֶשֶׁף

flame, flash, spark \= a sudden burst of brighly glowing light, whose source can be seen (like fire) or invisible (like lightning)

[JOB 5:7](https://ref.ly/Job5:7) · [PSA 78:48](https://ref.ly/Ps78:48) · [SNG 8:6](https://ref.ly/Song8:6) · [SNG 8:6](https://ref.ly/Song8:6)

Weapons

**Collocation:** רִשְׁפֵי־קֶשֶׁת

flashing arrows literally: flames of the bow; hence: \= pointed missile, shot from a bow; slender and straight in shape and moving swiftly; made out of wood and/or iron and used mainly for hunting and in warfare; ≈ in this context the focus is on the way the arrows flash through the sky

[PSA 76:4](https://ref.ly/Ps76:4)

Weak

plague, disease \= a destructive and deadly condition which affects nature

[DEU 32:24](https://ref.ly/Deut32:24) · [HAB 3:5](https://ref.ly/Hab3:5)

name

Names of People

Resheph \= son of Beriah, ancestor of Joshua, from the tribe of Ephraim

[1CH 7:25](https://ref.ly/1Chr7:25)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 5:7; Psalms 78:48; Song of Songs 8:6; Psalms 76:4; Deuteronomy 32:24; Habakkuk 3:5; 1 Chronicles 7:25


## רשׁשׁ (id: 006955000000000)

רשׁשׁ
=====

רשׁשׁ (H7567)

verb

Impact

to shatter, to crush \= causative action by which constructions such as towns, villages, and buildings are physically destroyed ► weakening a nation

[JER 5:17](https://ref.ly/Jer5:17) · [MAL 1:4](https://ref.ly/Mal1:4)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 5:17; Malachi 1:4


## רֶשֶׁת (id: 006956000000000)

רֶשֶׁת
======

רֶשֶׁת (H7568)

noun f · ירשׁ

Traps

net \= net of unknown size and shape; ► used for hunting birds and other animals, and also for fishing; ≈ associated with aggression and control

## רתח (id: 006958000000000)

רתח
===

verb · רֶתַח

Hot

[EZK 24:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:5)

Grieve

**Collocation:** מֵעִים רתח

to be in turmoil literally: (one's) inner parts are boiling; hence: \= process by which humans go through a phase of strong grief and distress

[JOB 30:27](https://ref.ly/Job30:27)

Unsteady

to cause to churn \= causative action by which a large animal causes water to start bubbling as if it is boiling
